 Any Facebook page has a rating system
 pej admin chaahe to ise public kar saktaa he yaa hataa saktaa he

 yah star reating hoti he or isamen 1 se lekar 4 star tak hote hai
 The star rating of the page depends on how many users have given so many stars
 udhaaharan ke taur par zyaadaatar yugers is pej ko 1 star de rahe hai to yahaan sirf ek blue star dikhegaa
